Page 7

The US Labor Strike Situation Worsens

Riots and Bloodshed Occur

National Guard Mobilized to Assist Police in Maintaining Order

The Strike Threatens to Extend Indefinitely

Sellersville, Rhode Island The labor strike here became increasingly serious today. Fierce battles broke out around the cotton mills, injuring 142 people, including 18 police officers. Although the cotton mills were protected by a large number of police, the crowds gathered in increasing numbers, eventually surging forward, breaking through the sentry line, and pushing down the factory gates. 360 soldiers and police officers were beaten by the crowds. The rioters even attempted to set fire to and destroy the factory. Fortunately, 300 artillerymen arrived at the factory in an emergency, and the crowds, seeing that they were no match, retreated. All the soldiers and police officers had orders not to fire under any circumstances, so they only used batons and tear gas to resist the rioters. (Reuters dispatch on the 12th)

Sellersville, Rhode Island Demonstrations and riots by strikers today resulted in three people being shot and injured by the police, including one woman. The strikers, disregarding warnings, gathered a large number of people and rushed to a factory to destroy the small room occupied by the gatekeepers. Although the police used batons to disperse them many times, they scattered and gathered again until firearms were used, and the crowds dispersed. The police claimed that they fired only for self-defense, as they could not have broken the siege otherwise and would have been subdued by the rioters. Since this case occurred, the strikers have been very angry. There are now 2,000 police officers stationed at the factory to prevent the strikers from continuing their attacks. Another 200 National Guard troops have been urgently summoned to assist the police in maintaining order. (Reuters dispatch on the 11th)

(Washington) The American Federation of Labor announced that it will provide economic assistance to striking workers. Therefore, the textile workers' strike seems likely to extend indefinitely tonight. Federation President Green told the Associated Press that the various unions have unanimously agreed to do their best to provide assistance. There are 4 million people affiliated with the Federation. If each person donates $5, there will be $20 million. At 6:00 PM tonight, Textile Workers Union Vice President Gorman stated that since the capitalists have rejected the union's public proposals, the labor side will not be responsible for any riots that may occur in the future. Therefore, the situation is worsening. Gorman issued an urgent plea today, requesting the capitalists to accept a "temporary ceasefire" before 6:00 PM, that is, all factories temporarily stop work and wait for a public judgment. Now, riots have occurred in various places, and workers have clashed with soldiers and police, injuring many people. Factories in various places are protected by the National Guard. In North Carolina, 19 factories resumed work yesterday under the protection of the military. (National Telegram on the 11th)

Japanese Sailors

Brewing a General Strike

Demanding Wage Increases and Improved Treatment

(Tokyo) While the Tokyo streetcar workers' strike has not ended, there is talk of a strike by 100,000 sailors. The labor unions of Nippon Yusen Kaisha and Dalian Steamship Company have proposed demands for improved treatment and wages, and have threatened to declare a general strike on the 23rd of this month if their demands are not met. (Reuters dispatch on the 12th)

Japanese Count Hijikata, Pro-Russian, Deprived of Peerage

(Tokyo) Writer Hijikata Yushi, also known as Count Hijikata Hisayoshi, has become a problem due to his speech in the Soviet Union some time ago. The Imperial Household Ministry's plan for the count's punishment is scheduled to begin discussion around the 20th of this month. As a result of convening a deliberation committee, it seems that a method has been determined to revoke Hijikata's peerage and impose a removal from the family. (Nikkan News dispatch on the 12th)

Japan Reforming Governance Organs in Manchuria

Opposing Okada's Compromise Proposal

The Kwantung Agency Prepares for Mass Resignation

The Fate of the Colonial Affairs Ministry Becomes a Question

The Military Negotiates with the Government

(Tokyo) According to a telegram from Lushun, regarding the reform of the governance organs in Manchuria, the government's compromise proposal completely disregards the Colonial Affairs Ministry's original plan. Therefore, the 15,000 staff members of the Kwantung Agency system, which maintains the Colonial Affairs Ministry's plan, from bureau chiefs to servants, have decided to resign en masse. Currently, they are collecting letters of resignation. The Colonial Affairs Ministry itself, which had previously been silent and attached importance to this matter, was greatly stimulated after receiving this letter. A part of it had already been shaken, and as a result, the entire ministry will be greatly shaken. (Dentsu dispatch on the 12th)

(Tokyo) Prime Minister Okada is convinced that the government's private proposal regarding the reform of the governance organs in Manchuria was determined after exchanging opinions with the authorities concerned. Therefore, there is no room for major changes in this private proposal. The content of the private proposal is based on the army's plan, and the outer form adopts the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' plan. It is the best plan. Therefore, although the Colonial Affairs Ministry's plan is sacrificed, Prime Minister Okada, who also concurrently serves as the Colonial Affairs Minister, is confident that he can make them understand. Another meeting of the related cabinet members will be held in two or three days, and it will definitely be resolved satisfactorily. (Dentsu dispatch on the 12th)

(Tokyo) Although it is expected that there will be twists and turns in the Japanese government's reform of the governing organs in Manchuria, it seems that the reform will eventually be implemented. At that time, all the powers of the Colonial Affairs Ministry over Manchuria (except for colonial affairs) will be eliminated. The rest will only govern the Governor-Generals and Chiefs of Taiwan, Korea, and Sakhalin. The amount of affairs will be drastically reduced, and it could be abolished. However, if the colonial rice control issue occurs, there must be a Colonial Affairs Minister to contact the central government, and if it is abolished temporarily, it is feared that it will arouse opposition from all the officials of the ministry. Therefore, the leaders of the current government have decided only to reform its organization, but the timing must wait for an appropriate opportunity. (Hualian dispatch on the 12th)

(Tokyo) Regarding the government's compromise proposal for the reform of the resident organs in Manchuria, the Army Ministry has requested revisions to (1) the establishment of the status of Ambassador Extraordinary and Plenipotentiary and the special official system regarding qualifications, and (2) the issue of the Manchuria Affairs Bureau under the management of the Prime Minister. Army Minister Hayashi met with Prime Minister Okada on the morning of the 12th and explained the army's opinions on this matter. (Nikkan News dispatch on the 12th)

(Tokyo) Regarding the reform of the resident organs in Manchuria, as a result of the meeting between Prime Minister Okada and Army Minister Hayashi on the morning of the 12th, there is a dawn of a satisfactory resolution. Regarding the future request from the army to supplement and correct the government's compromise proposal, the relevant authorities can conduct further negotiations. After determining the final plan, it is scheduled to be decided and endorsed at the regular cabinet meeting on the 14th. (Nikkan News dispatch on the 12th)

Content of the Compromise Proposal

(Tokyo) Regarding the reform of the resident organs in Manchuria, the content of the compromise proposal still in the hands of Prime Minister Okada is as follows: (1) The Ambassador Extraordinary and Plenipotentiary resident in Manchuria is a purely diplomatic official, concurrently held by the commander of the Kwantung Army, and is under the orders of the Minister of Foreign Affairs. (1) The Ambassador Extraordinary and Plenipotentiary is granted administrative supervisory power, which is stipulated by single-line imperial decrees. This supervisory power belongs to the Prime Minister's command system. (1) Under the Ambassador Extraordinary and Plenipotentiary, a counselor is appointed to handle diplomatic affairs, and at the same time, an administrative affairs director-general is appointed as an administrative official, who is under the command system of the Prime Minister through the Ambassador Extraordinary and Plenipotentiary. The Governor of Kwantung Prefecture and the ministers appointed by imperial decree are under the command of the Prime Minister through the administrative affairs director-general of the Ambassador Extraordinary and Plenipotentiary. (1) A Manchuria Affairs Bureau is established in the Cabinet, and the Manchuria Affairs Participation Conference is directly under the Prime Minister. (1) The Director-General of the Manchuria Affairs Bureau is, in principle, a civil official appointed as a personal office. (1) The Manchuria Affairs Participation Conference appoints the heads of the relevant ministries, including the Army, Foreign Affairs, Colonial Affairs, and Finance ministries. (1) The Colonial Affairs Minister conducts overseas colonial immigration matters through the consulates under the orders of the Foreign Minister. In addition, regarding the government's reform of the resident organs in Manchuria, in order to control the industrial economy of Japan and Manchukuo, a Japan-Manchukuo Economic Conference is established, stationed permanently in Changchun, and organized by the same kind of committee members appointed by the governments of the two countries. (Dentsu dispatch on the 12th)

Key Points of the Military's Claims

Army Commander Concurrently Serves as Ambassador Extraordinary and Plenipotentiary

(Tokyo) The Army convened a meeting of its leaders at 9:00 PM last night regarding the government's compromise proposal for the reform of the resident organs in Manchuria. As a result of the negotiations, it was decided to revise the following points, which will be presented to Prime Minister Okada after obtaining the understanding of the non-official military councilors today. Namely, (1) As in the government's proposal, the Ambassador Extraordinary and Plenipotentiary resident in Manchuria is the same as other general ambassadors, although he has the form of concurrently handling administrative matters. However, this does not conform to the reality of Manchuria. Therefore, a special official system should be established with the ambassador as the center, and administrative affairs should also be the natural powers of the ambassador. The ambassador should be the official agency for administrative diplomacy. (1) According to the government's proposal, the director of the Manchuria Affairs Bureau can be filled by the Colonial Affairs Minister. However, this is contrary to the actual requirements of Manchuria, making the reform of the resident organs in Manchuria meaningless. Therefore, it should be stipulated that the director cannot be filled by the Colonial Affairs Minister or the heads of the Colonial Affairs Ministry, but should be filled by an active-duty officer. That is, the director-general of affairs under the ambassador should also be filled by the chief of staff of the Kwantung Army or an active-duty officer. (Dentsu dispatch on the 12th)

(Tokyo) The Army is quite dissatisfied with the government's proposal for the reform of the resident organs in Manchuria. The key points of the Army's claims are as follows: (1) The right to petition of the Ambassador Extraordinary and Plenipotentiary should be returned to the Army Minister. (2) It must be clearly stated that the Ambassador Extraordinary and Plenipotentiary is concurrently held by a military officer. (3) It must be clearly stated that the Director-General of the Manchuria Affairs Bureau is filled by a military officer. It is difficult to agree to the government's proposal that it should be filled by a civil official in principle. (4) The Chief of Staff of the Kwantung Army should be appointed as the Director-General of Affairs. It is noteworthy that the Army's plan calls for the commander of the army to concurrently serve as the Ambassador Extraordinary and Plenipotentiary and have thorough and permanent power. If the government and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs do not object to this request, a comprehensive solution may be obtained at the cabinet meeting on the 14th. (Dentsu dispatch on the 12th)

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs Proposes a Counterproposal

Arguing for Unified Command of the Police

(Tokyo) After yesterday's three-minister meeting on the reform of the resident organs in Manchuria ended, Foreign Minister Hirota convened a meeting of the heads of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. Although the government's proposal was generally approved, there were still dissatisfactions regarding detailed matters such as police unification. Therefore, a counterproposal was made and presented to Prime Minister Okada on the 12th. That is, the government's proposal places the command and supervision of consular police and affiliated police under the ambassador, while the command system of the former belongs to the Minister of Foreign Affairs and the latter belongs to the Prime Minister. This lacks unity. In the future, the attached areas of the South Manchuria Railway must be returned, so the command and supervision of the two police forces should be unified under the Minister of Foreign Affairs and managed by the Ambassador Extraordinary and Plenipotentiary. (Dentsu dispatch on the 12th)

(Tokyo) In addition to advocating that this ambassador directly supervise the administrative police power of the South Manchuria Railway attached areas, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs maintains its attitude based on the following policies: (1) Respect the independence of Manchukuo. (2) The establishment of various policies must consider the inseparable relationship between Japan and Manchukuo. (3) The current three-in-one system is a temporary measure. In the future, separate the three items of diplomacy, military affairs, and economy. Military and government officials should not concurrently serve as the ambassador resident in Manchuria. (Nikkan News dispatch on the 12th)

Eliminating Powers in Manchuria

The Colonial Affairs Ministry Expresses Absolute Opposition

(Tokyo) Because its powers in Manchuria are almost completely eliminated, the Colonial Affairs Ministry absolutely opposes the compromise proposal. Therefore, how Prime Minister Okada's proposed compromise proposal will turn out cannot be predicted. (Nikkan News dispatch on the 12th)

Severe Drought in Japan

Area Spanning Twelve Prefectures

Loss of One Hundred Million Yuan

(Tokyo) According to statistics from the Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry, as of the end of August, the drought-stricken areas include Chiba, Okayama, Kagawa, Ehime, Fukuoka, Saga, Nagasaki, Kumamoto, Oita, Miyazaki, Kagoshima, and other twelve prefectures, covering an area of 326,000 hectares. The harvest has been reduced by approximately 3,171,000 stones, and the total damage is approximately 100 million yen. Because of the urgent need for relief, the Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry will request the Ministry of Finance to spend relief funds from the second reserve fund. (Dentsu dispatch on the 12th)

Norway Boycotts Japanese Goods

(Tokyo) According to a telegram received by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs from the Minister to Norway, Shiratori, today, the Norwegian government has decided to implement an import quota system for Japanese rubber boots and ceramics, which will be implemented from March 1st of this year, using 1931 or 1928 as the benchmark, and the import volume from March 1st to February 28th of next year has been determined. However, since March of this year, the aforementioned two Japanese goods have exceeded their limit, which has greatly impacted Japanese merchants. Foreign Minister Hirota plans to instruct Minister Shiratori by telegram to negotiate with the Norwegian government. (Hualian dispatch on the 12th)

German Trade Control

Promulgating Five New Orders to Revise Various Regulations

Establishing 25 Bureaus to Manage Import and Export Goods

(Berlin) Germany's foreign trade is about to be completely reorganized. The authorities have now issued five orders involving cargo transportation, raw material control, and amendments to existing laws regarding foreign currency control. From September 24th, Germany's imports and exports, as well as agriculture, industry, and commerce, will be managed by 25 control bureaus. Importers who have not obtained a foreign currency permit may find it difficult to obtain the necessary foreign currency within a considerable period of time. This permit will only be issued to legitimate importers in the future. According to officials, the new regulations hint to importers that a commodity exchange system will be developed on a larger scale. (China News Agency dispatch on the 11th)

(Berlin) The new measures taken by Acting Minister of Economic Affairs Schacht to regulate foreign trade were officially announced today by Chai Nuofu, Director of the Economic Ministry, on behalf of Schacht. The various measures are divided into five orders, two of which are currently being implemented. The main points are listed as follows: (2) The number of raw material control agencies has increased to 25, and all imported goods are controlled by the government. (2) The currency required for paying for imported goods in the past is distributed by a special management

London Gold Price: This morning's London gold price was 140 shillings, 5 and a half pence, up 2 pence.

Sterling-Dollar: The London foreign exchange market was quiet this morning. There was little trading except for a short period. The opening exchange rate for Sterling-Dollar was 5 dollars, 03 and 75 cents, the same as yesterday's closing rate. Cotton and Wheat

American Cotton: The New York cotton market opened down 56 points, due to favorable weather, poor Liverpool telegraphs, and continued uncertainty in the stock market. Although the cotton market's fundamentals were still sound, the market was chaotic before noon. Near-term contracts rose 6 points, while far-term contracts fell 1 point. After continued mixed trading, the December contract rose 6 points at 10:40, while the March contract price remained unchanged from the opening.

Indian Cotton: The Bombay cotton market initially fell due to large-scale selling by speculators, but stabilized at closing due to purchases by European exporters. The closing price for the April-May contract of Luo Qu cotton was 220 rupees, 25, up 1 rupee, 25.

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market also rose slightly today. At 1 PM, the October contract price was 6.91, up 1 point.

Rubber

New York: Rubber opened down 3 to 5 points. Continued declines before noon. Recent prices indicated a drop of 9 to 10 points.

Steel industry operations in Chicago increased slightly, reaching 24% of its production capacity. The factors unfavorable to the market were: (1) Labor unrest continued to cause concern; (2) Government bonds were weak; (3) The Democratic Party's victory in the Maine election was disappointing, as it was seen as a sign of support for government policies. This morning, the stock market opened quietly, with limited price fluctuations. The overall trend was mostly bullish. US Steel stock rose 1 point, but buyers were cautious and unwilling to take risks. Therefore, the recent atmosphere in the stock market remains uncertain, and it seems that the market will continue to be volatile. New York stock market prices are as follows:

Strict Prohibition of Gambling in Fuzhou

Flower Association Gambling Dens Gradually Decreasing

Fuzhou Correspondence: The Fujian Provincial Government, in order to strictly prohibit Taiwanese from running flower associations, issued a proclamation yesterday stating: "The operation of flower associations has long been strictly prohibited. In the past, the main offenders were severely punished. However, over time, people have become lax, and recently, unscrupulous individuals in Fuzhou City have disregarded the ban and secretly operated these associations. Ignorant and foolish people pursue and gamble on them, recklessly breaking the law, which is heartbreaking. Recently, the Nanchang Headquarters has approved the Regulations on Punishing Special Types of Gambling in this province, which this government has promulgated and made known. Flower associations are one of the special types of gambling, and the penalties are very severe, ranging from imprisonment to execution. Heavy penalties are used to restore order and reverse the declining trend. Considering that we are all citizens, we should seek legitimate occupations. Gaining temporary small profits leads to inescapable legal consequences, which is punishable and pitiable. Therefore, this proclamation is re-emphasized. Everyone must repent, immediately close down the associations, and seek legitimate employment to avoid criminal charges. If they continue to be stubborn and regard the ban as a mere formality, this chairman will order the enforcement agencies to punish them according to the law without any leniency. As for military, police, and civil servants who harbor such activities, they will also be punished to the fullest extent according to the regulations." Regarding the Public Security Bureau, from the 3rd to the 5th, the police and detectives arrested more than 50 Chinese partners in various foreign card flower association gambling dens. The authorities now plan to transfer those with serious offenses to the Military Law Section of the Security Office for trial, while those with minor offenses will be dealt with by the Judicial Section of the Public Security Bureau. The number of flower association gambling dens in the city has decreased from more than 30 to 4 as of the 5th. However, there are very few gamblers, making it difficult for the dens to survive. As a result, the Taiwanese vagrants have become extremely resentful of the police and detectives. For days, they have been in groups of three or five, carrying pistols and bayonets, provoking and committing violence in Nandaomen and Ximen Street. However, the authorities have made great efforts to prevent this from happening. (6th)

Confucian Clan Representatives Suggest

Building a Museum and Library in Qufu

To Display Ancient Carriages, Clothing, and Ritual Objects

And Reprinting the Confucian Mansion's Collection

Jinan Correspondence: In order to honor Confucius, the Central Government has issued an order nationwide to hold commemorative conferences on Confucius's birthday. Ye Chucang was also dispatched to Qufu to preside over the ceremonies. The grandeur of the ceremonies was unprecedented. From the provincial side, the Director of the Department of Civil Affairs Li Shuchun and the Director of the Department of Education He Siyuan also went to participate in the Confucius memorial ceremony. While in Qufu, they saw that the Kuiwen Pavilion of the Confucius Temple was damaged and many musical instruments were in disrepair. After returning to Jinan, they proposed at the provincial government's political affairs meeting to repair the Kuiwen Pavilion of the Confucius Temple, display all kinds of carriages, clothing, and ritual objects, and repair ancient musical instruments. After the two proposals were passed, they are now being prepared for implementation. The Confucian clansmen of Qufu specially dispatched Kong Fanzheng and Kong Lingcan to Jinan to express their gratitude and discuss the preservation of ancient documents. According to the Confucian clan's opinion, it is planned to build a museum to display carriages, clothing, ritual objects, etc., for the viewing of Chinese and foreign visitors to Qufu, and to build a library to display the ancient books collected in the Confucian Mansion. The plan coincides with the proposals passed by the provincial government. In addition, it is planned to organize and publish books. The ancient books stored in the Confucian Mansion that have already been engraved and printed were printed once during the Guangxu period of Sun Qing. The printing plates have been piled up for decades. It is now planned to reprint them. Many of the books have not been seen outside. There are also many musical scores. Kong Yunting, the author of the Peach Blossom Fan, wrote many books, and it is planned to engrave and print those that have not been printed. However, this kind of work is very expensive. According to the Confucian clan's opinion, it is planned to ask the provincial government to advance some funds. After the books are printed and sold, the proceeds will be used to repay the provincial government. The Director of the Provincial Library, Wang Xiantang, strongly supports this matter because it is related to the circulation of ancient books. He is currently in contact with them, and it is possible that it will be realized.

In addition, the Confucian clan genealogy has not been revised for many years. Because there are many branches of the clan, the work is not easy. Recently, Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi advocated for the resumption of the revision, and the Kong clan can donate 100,000 yuan to help it succeed. According to calculations, the required funds are no less than 200,000, which is almost there. As soon as the preparations are complete, the revision will begin. (11th)

Anhui Province Relief Committee

Requests Allocation of Agricultural Relief Funds to Farmers

—To Provide Funds for Planting After the Disaster—

Anqing Correspondence: The drought in Anhui Province this year is severe, many times worse than the flood of 1931. The Provincial Disaster Relief Committee plans to allocate all the funds, including principal and interest, totaling more than 1 million yuan, that were previously allocated to Anhui Province for American wheat by the National Government Flood Relief Committee, back to farmers to provide funds for planting after the disaster. Yesterday, a special letter was sent to the Provincial Government, requesting that it telegraph the National Economic Council to order it to do so in order to provide relief. The original letter is as follows: "Regarding the previous suggestion from this committee to your government to request that the funds from the China International Famine Relief Commission for agricultural relief in Anhui Province be allocated in full, or to specially borrow 300,000 yuan to repair the breached dikes, letters and telegrams have been exchanged, but the allocation has not yet been made. This is because the drought in our province this year is even more severe than the floods of previous years. The disaster area covers as many as 48 counties, with tens of millions of disaster victims. Not only is their current livelihood cut off, but also the seeds for planting after this autumn are nowhere to be found. This is not only related to local production, but also to local safety. Looking ahead, we cannot help but shudder. Therefore, it has been jointly decided to suggest that the more than 1 million yuan, including the wheat price and interest, of the 11,800 tons of American wheat previously allocated to Anhui Province by the National Government Flood Relief Committee and stored by the China International Famine Relief Commission should be allocated to the farmers for planting after the disaster. This is not inconsistent with the original agricultural relief plan. It seems reasonable to use the original funds for relieving the farmers of Anhui to continue to relieve the farmers of Anhui. However, the autumn is coming soon, and the matter is urgent. Therefore, we specially request that you investigate and promptly telegraph the National Economic Council to order the China International Famine Relief Commission to quickly allocate the principal and interest of more than 1 million yuan of the aforementioned agricultural relief funds back to our province for relief, which is immeasurably anticipated." (September 9)

Zhejiang Province's Telecommunications Network Fully Completed

Long-distance Trunk and Branch Lines Total 4,500 Kilometers

A Total of 59 Long-distance Branch Offices in the Province

In addition to building railways and highways, the Zhejiang Provincial Government has also been keen on building a telecommunications network in recent years. Under the supervision of Director of the Department of Construction Zeng Yangfu and the diligent management of Director of the Zhejiang Provincial Telephone Bureau Zhao Zengjue, the province's long-distance telecommunications network is now accessible in all directions, spreading throughout the counties, making it the best in the country. The long-distance telephone lines originally laid in Zhejiang Province were mainly for communicating military information, so they were mostly hung on telegraph poles. The engineering was simple. After the National Government established its capital in Nanjing in 1927, the Department of Construction drafted a basic plan for long-distance telephones. In March 1928, the Zhejiang Provincial Long-Distance Telephone Bureau was established. All facilities were carried out according to the basic plan, dividing the province into eight major trunk lines. In addition to the trunk lines, there are branch lines, village lines, and border defense lines. Now, 4,500 kilometers of long-distance trunk and branch lines, 1,270 kilometers of village lines, and 550 kilometers of border defense lines have been completed. The points reached by the trunk and branch lines are all designated as central points. The current central points are Hangzhou, Lanxi, Yongjia, Linhai, Ningbo, Jiaxing, Lishui, and other exchange centers in seven locations. The centers are all connected by direct lines. Of the 75 counties in the province, all except Dinghai and Nantian have telephone service. Dinghai and Nantian are isolated in the sea, and water lines are currently being planned. However, Dinghai already has a radio station for reporting, and Nantian is also planning to set up a radio station to remedy the situation. All trunk lines are made of copper, and the standards are very strict, so the transmission is very clear. Currently, there are a total of 59 long-distance branch offices and 185 long-distance agency offices in the province. News between the counties can be transmitted throughout the province in an instant, which is very convenient. Now that the Southeast Transportation Exhibition is about to open, the Telephone Bureau is also planning various telecommunications in the scenic areas, which will make communication even smoother. However, the basic project is the long-distance telephone service in 73 counties. The following is a summary:

Hangzhou-Changxing Line: From Hangzhou through Wukang, Wuxing, and Changxing to the Jiangsu Province border, the total length is 167.62 kilometers, with four branch lines: (1) Wukang-Mogan Branch Line: From Wukang to Mogan Mountain, the total length is 14.40 kilometers. (2) Huzhou-Jiaxing Branch Line: From Wuxing through Nanxun to Jiaxing, the total length is 80.64 kilometers. (3) Changxing-Si'an Branch Line: From Changxing to Si'an, the total length is 27.65 kilometers. (4) Wuxing-Xiaofeng Branch Line: From Wuxing through Anji to Xiaofeng, the total length is 78.92 kilometers.

(2) Shaoxing-Taizhou Branch Line: From Shaoxing through Sheng County and Xinchang to Taizhou, the total length is 205.63 kilometers.

Longyou-Wenzhou Line: From Longyou, Suichang, Songyang, Lishui, Qingtian to Yongjia, with one double line, the total length is 294.91 kilometers, with two branch lines: (1) Yongjia-Aojiang Branch Line: From Yongjia through Pingyang to Aojiang, the total length is 57.60 kilometers. (2) Yunhe-Taishun Branch Line: From Yunhe through Jingning to Taishun, the total length is 91.59 kilometers. Hangzhou-Chuzhou Line: From Hangzhou through Zhuji, Yiwu, Jinhua, with one double line; from Jinhua through Yongkang, Jinyun to Lishui, with two double lines, the total length is 451.57 kilometers, with two branch lines: (1) Yiwu-Dongyang Branch Line: From Yiwu to Dongyang, the total length is 19.58 kilometers. (2) Yiwu-Pujiang Branch Line: From Yiwu to Pujiang, the total length is 27.65 kilometers. Hangzhou-Fengjing Line: From Hangzhou through Chang'an, Chongde, Tongxiang, Jiaxing, Fengjing to Longhua, with two double lines, the total length is 419.34 kilometers, with three branch lines: (1) Chang'an-Jiaxing Branch Line: From Chang'an through Haining, Xieqiao, Xiashi, Wangdian to Jiaxing, the total length is 65.09 kilometers. (2) Jiashan-Zhapu Branch Line: From Jiashan through Pinghu to Zhapu, the total length is 36.29 kilometers. (3) Hangzhou-Deqing Branch Line: From Hangzhou through Tangqi to Deqing, the total length is 48.39 kilometers. Hangzhou-Changhua Line: From Hangzhou through Yuhang, Lin'an, Yuqian to Changhua, the total length is 114.05 kilometers. In addition to the long-distance telephone lines mentioned above, the Zhejiang Provincial Telephone Bureau also operates automatic telephone systems in Hangzhou and urban telephone systems in Lanxi, Jinhua, Haimen, Sheng County, Lishui, Cixi, Yuhang, Mogan Mountain, Changshan, Wuzhen and other cities and towns to benefit the people. Other counties, such as Zhuji and Yongkang, are also actively planning to establish them.

Beijing-Hankou Railway Bureau

Plans to Repair the Yellow River Railway Bridge

Railway Revenue Exceeds 300,000 per Month, Reserves for Construction

Decided on Reorganization Steps, Pay Attention to Driving Safety

Beijing Correspondence: The news of the Beijing-Hankou Railway borrowing funds and expanding has attracted much attention from all walks of life. Here are the details: The Beijing-Hankou Railway has been affected by military operations for many years, and the sleepers, bridges, and rails have been severely damaged and urgently need repair and replacement. However, due to limited finances, it has been difficult to achieve this. In recent years, the bureau has implemented reorganization in both material and spiritual ways, within the possible scope, sweeping away the old habits of the past and engaging in thrift. It is estimated that more than 300,000 yuan can be saved each month, stored monthly to finance construction, and progress is made step by step according to the urgency of the project. It is expected that the entire railway can be restored to its complete state in seven years. It is now planned to use the more than 3 million yuan saved each year to reorganize the equipment of locomotives and vehicles.

However, in recent years, due to the influence of the environment, there are many outstanding debts that also need to be repaid. However, with this deposit of more than 3 million yuan per year, it is expected that the miscellaneous debts can be cleared in two or three years. There are also considerable measures for opening up revenue sources, and future construction can be carried out more actively. As for its reorganization steps: (1) Pay attention to driving safety; (2) Strive to increase efficiency; (3) Regarding the comfort of passengers and the equipment of stations along the line, especially the repair of the Yellow River Railway Bridge, which is urgent, because the bridge foundation is already too loose to be used. It has been decided to start construction this year.

Regarding the rumor that the Beijing-Hankou Railway borrowed 30 million yuan, according to Chen Yanjiong and Zou Anzhong of the Beijing-Hankou Railway, not only did the Ministry of Railways and this railway have no such intention, but there was no so-called contract signed. It is unknown where this statement came from. Such rumors are absolutely untrue. (Shenshi News Agency)

Shanxi Province Strictly Prevents Shaanxi Bandits

Shilou and Linxian Counties Send Urgent Telegraphs to Warn

The Pacification Headquarters Dispatches Troops to Block and Attack

Taiyuan Correspondence: The bandits in the counties along the river in eastern Shaanxi have been incited by the bandit leader Wang Ermei and have become increasingly rampant in recent times. Branches have been set up in all counties and villages, coercing villagers to commit evil together. If they do not obey, they will be brutally killed. The people of eastern Shaanxi are suffering from trampling, and hundreds of people flee across the river to Shanxi every day to seek refuge. The authorities in the counties of western Shanxi are afraid that the bandits may sneak in and carry out activities in Shanxi, so they are strictly inspecting at the ferry crossings, only allowing women and children to land. All adult men who are suspicious are refused entry. However, because the people of eastern Shaanxi have either been drawn into bandit lairs, or been brutally killed, or have fled with their young and old, the source of supplies has been cut off. Therefore, there is an attempt to cross the river to the east and plunder in Shanxi. According to the report from Li Shude, the magistrate of Shilou County, on the 3rd of this month, the Shaanxi bandits are close to the riverbank, building protective works to cross the river, and dozens of bandits have crossed the river by boat. Although they were repelled by our army, they are still lurking in the nearby mountains, ready to make trouble. The magistrate of Linxian County also reported that more than a dozen villages, including Qianzhuang, in Mizhi County, Shaanxi Province, across the river, have been occupied by the bandit leader Liu Zishan, leading four to five hundred bandits, separated from western Shanxi by only one river. The provincial defense is crucial, and it is urgent to find a way to prevent it. After receiving the telegram, the provincial authorities, in addition to telegraphing the Suiyuan Garrison to dispatch the Cai Regiment of the 71st Division, which was building a car road in Yangmingbao, to block them, the provincial government also telegraphed the magistrates of Pianguan, Hequ, Baode, Xingxian, Lanshi, Zhongyang, Yonghe, Daning, Jixian, and Xiangning counties along the river today to cooperate with the military and police to strictly prevent them. Recent News on the Repair of the Seawall in Songjiang

The Department of Construction believes that the seawalls in the three counties of Jiangnan, Taicang, Baoshan, and Songjiang are gradually collapsing and urgently need to be repaired. Therefore, it allocated more than 500,000 yuan in construction costs and dispatched engineer Chen Shoulian to supervise the repairs. On the one hand, it hired elders from each county as supervisors to supervise the work. The seawall in this county was repaired by Bureau of Construction Director Xu Baikui in 1926 after requesting funds. It was built with cement, but the embankment surface was filled with gravel, causing water leakage and accumulation, which easily damaged the embankment body. This time, the Jinshanwei area will repair three sections of the project, which will cost more than 70,000 yuan. Shen Siqi and Min Ruizhi were hired as supervisors, and Wu Boyang and Zhou Mengxiong were hired as assistant supervisors. At the end of last month, a section chief of the Department of Construction, together with supervisors Zhu Kaipan, Chou Hongjing, and Ping, personally inspected the Jinshanwei seawall construction site. At the beginning of the month, assistant supervisors Wu Boyang and Zhou Mengxiong accompanied engineer Chen to inspect the area. The first and second sections of the project have been completed, and the third section of the embankment surface is currently under construction. On the afternoon of the 10th, they went to No. 70 Renji Road, Shanghai, to hold a supervisors' meeting. Taicang members Zhu and Hong, Baoshan members Jin and Zhao, and Songjiang Shen Siqi and Wu Boyang attended. They all believed that the drawback of this embankment was that the subcontracting did not conform to the detailed rules for material handling, and the sloppiness of the project was secondary. It was decided to have Shen Siqi draft a letter to urge the Director of the Department of Construction to pay attention.

Local News

Sun Ke Returned to Shanghai Yesterday Morning

He Spoke Freely About the International Situation, Believing That Japan and Russia Would Not Immediately Go to War

He Will Go to Nanjing Tonight to Attend the Plenary Session of the Legislative Yuan

Sun Ke, the President of the Legislative Yuan, took advantage of the Legislative Yuan's vacation last month to go to Honolulu with his family and Yu Ming, the Director of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Shanghai Office, to escape the summer heat and meet with US President Roosevelt. He returned to Shanghai on the Changxing Company's Empress of Japan yesterday morning around 8:00 AM. Mayor Wu and others went to welcome him. Mr. Sun is scheduled to go to Nanjing tonight to attend the Legislative Yuan's plenary session on the 14th. Details are recorded as follows:

Welcoming at the Pier

The Empress of Japan entered the port at 5:00 AM yesterday morning. At 6:00 AM, it docked at the Pudong Changxing Wharf. All the welcoming personnel gathered at the new Customs Wharf in the early morning and took the Yuebao and Jinghui small steamships to welcome him. Those present included Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Vice Minister of the Interior Fu Rulin, Secretary Liu Weichi, Central Committee Member Zhang Huichang, Legislators Liang Hancao, Ma Chaojun, Wu Jingxiong, Zhang Zhiben, Zhong Tianxin, Chen Jianru, Security Chief Yang Hu, Police Chief Wen Hongen, Zhao Tiegang and Li Rongyao of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Shanghai Office, Jiaotong University President Li Zhao huan, and more than 100 relatives and friends of Mr. Sun. Mr. Sun and the crowd boarded the Yuebao small steamship and arrived at the new Customs Wharf at around 8:00 AM. He immediately boarded his car and returned to his private residence on Columbia Road to rest. Mr. Sun brought back many Honolulu dance wreaths from Honolulu and gave them to the welcoming staff. Therefore, both men and women were wearing a wreath, which was quite interesting.

Meeting with the US President

Mr. Sun told reporters in the cabin that he had taken advantage of the Legislative Yuan's recess to go to Honolulu with his family to escape the summer heat. Now that the hot summer has passed, he is returning by boat. After a short stay in Shanghai, he will take the night train to Nanjing on the 13th to preside over the first meeting of the Legislative Yuan after the recess on the 14th. The constitutional issue will not be discussed at the meeting. During his stay in Honolulu, he met with US President Roosevelt in passing, but it was purely an ordinary meeting and did not involve any political issues.

International Situation

According to various reports, the relationship between Japan and the United States has become more tense due to the tension between Japan and Russia. Mr. Sun said that during his month-long stay in Honolulu, he did not see any changes in the relationship between Japan and the United States. However, when traveling back and forth through Japan, he only knew that the Japanese authorities were very active in preparing for military affairs, especially air defense equipment. However, according to his observations, any country is now actively preparing for air defense, but it is difficult to say whether its air defense equipment will be as effective as desired once war breaks out in the future. As for the issue between Japan and Russia, although the situation between the two countries is tense, the sale of the Middle East Road seems to have broken down, but it is expected that the war will not break out immediately because of this. Furthermore, although the negotiations on the Middle East Road are on the verge of collapse, the authorities of both countries still hope to delay the outbreak of war with the issue of the Middle East Road. The 15th session of the League of Nations has now opened. It is firmly believed that the League of Nations will still adhere to its original position on the issue of the puppet organization and will always deny it. As for the British industrial inspection team's visit to Northeast China, the team was organized by British businessmen and not by the British government. It is based on the principle of "smelling meat but not eating it." As for the Anglo-Japanese alliance and the conclusion of secret agreements, it is also the air that the Japanese side is eager to release. Although the rumors are rife, the United Kingdom has not had this intention so far.

US Economy

Mr. Sun continued to answer reporters' questions. Although he was not in Honolulu for a long time, he felt that although the United States was said to be better on the surface after the implementation of the recovery policy, in reality, there was no real improvement, and he felt that its difficulties were increasing at any time, such as the great drought and strikes. Under these circumstances, the advantages and disadvantages of the recovery policy in the trial run are still difficult to predict. At present, 25 out of 100 people in the United States rely on the government to maintain their lives. This alone can prove that the trial run of the US recovery policy has not achieved considerable results. As for the United States raising the price of silver and nationalizing silver, it is a policy of currency inflation. Silver is nationalized at 50.001 cents per ounce, but on the one hand, it is used as a reserve for issuing 1.20 yuan of banknotes per ounce, which proves that it is a currency inflation policy. At the same time, due to the United States raising the price of silver, speculators buy silver and export it for profit, which is of course a major disadvantage to our country's finances.

Fifth Plenary Session

Regarding the Central Government's preparations for the Fifth National Congress, Mr. Sun said that he had just arrived in the country and was not aware of the details, but he said that the opening of the Fifth National Congress will definitely not be extended any longer, which can be asserted. If the Southwest has proposals and legitimate reasons to state, they can be submitted to the Congress. The reason is that the Fifth National Congress cannot be opposed by anyone, which is very clear. Mr. Sun also said that he had not prepared for the proposals to the Congress because the opening date was still far away.

Special Survey of Domestic Goods Industry

(5) Ink Industry

The ink industry is developing with the cultural industry. Since the introduction of printing, European-made ink has been imported along with it. At first, there was only black ink, and then various colored inks were imported, mostly from Germany and Japan. During the European War, the source of ink was suddenly cut off, and Chinese people rushed to set up ink factories to manufacture it themselves. However, except for the Commercial Press, most of them had too little capital, and their output was small and without significant achievements. In recent years, they have gradually developed, and larger factories include Yonghe Industrial, Tongwen, and Lingsheng. Recently, we visited Mr. Ye Jiting, the factory director of Yonghe Industrial Company, and Mr. Qian Mengwei, the director of the ink department. After the visit, we had a conversation, which is briefly recorded as follows:

Mr. Qian said that there are generally three types of machines for manufacturing ink: rolling mill, grinder, and mixer. The raw materials for ink are generally varnish and color powder. The most common color powder is ink ash, and the varnish is mostly made by frying sesame oil from Yajiakou. The manufacturing ingredients are tung oil, sesame oil, red oil (mineral oil), pigment powder, ink ash, rosin, magnesium carbonate, varnish, etc. The manufacturing is still simple. First, the oil is made into varnish, and then it is mixed with ink ash or pigment powder, and then it is put on the machine for repeated mixing. Generally, high-quality ink needs to be rolled 15 to 18 times. Ink is used for four types: copperplate ink, lithographic ink, offset ink, and mimeograph ink. There are eight or nine companies in the industry, including Yonghe Industrial, Tongwen, Lingsheng, Junda, Gongsheng, and Yihua. There is no organization of the same industry association. Some are called domestic goods factories, but in fact, they sell imported ink, change the name, and claim to be domestic goods, so as to gain huge profits. Users do not distinguish between true and false, and only covet cheap prices, which greatly affects domestic goods ink. At present, the annual sales volume of domestic products is only 600,000 yuan, while the survey shows that the annual demand for ink is 9 million yuan, accounting for only one-fifteenth. If domestic goods manufacturers can research cheap and high-quality ink, increase capital, and produce in large quantities, it is not difficult to compete with Japanese goods. In terms of raw materials, except for colors, oils can all be obtained without waiting for foreign demand. Mr. Qian is a chemical expert. Recently, he has overcome various difficulties, and the ink he produces has been comparable to imported products, and all parties are happy to use it. However, Japanese goods are being dumped more and more fiercely, and merchants are willing to be accomplices and fuel the flames. Domestic goods ink always feels squeezed everywhere. Although there are no factories that have failed recently, the interest is also very small. It is hoped that all factories will concentrate on researching the improvement of products and the reduction of costs, or they may be able to drive out foreign goods and compete with them. Otherwise, they will fight each other, or be willing to sell Japanese goods, and there will be no good results in the industry in the future. Yonghe Ink Factory was founded in the 17th year of the Republic of China with a capital of 100,000 yuan. It has oil-making workshops, pigment workshops, and ink-making workshops on Minsheng Road, West Baoxing Road, Zhabei. All of them are equipped with the latest machinery, and all management is completely scientific. The products include rubber car ink, lithographic ink, letterpress ink, three-color plate ink, and printing ink. Among the domestic goods ink factories in Shanghai, the equipment is the most complete, and the factory is the first to be able to use domestic self-made varnish and self-made dry pigments. Factory director Ye Jiting is a Ph.D. in Chemistry from the University of Berlin, Germany. Director Qian Mengwei was the factory director of Sino-American Oil Factory. He has been studying pigments and ink with German Dr. Connisch for many years and has rich experience, so he can have this achievement. Mr. Qian said that the ink industry is not only related to culture and education, but also very helpful to industry. He is now uniting with his peers to cooperate thoroughly and strive for technological improvements, so as to defeat imported ink and recover this huge leak of 8.4 million yuan.

Overseas Chinese Returning from Korea

Talk About the Japanese Restriction on Overseas Chinese Entering Korea

Overseas Chinese Unanimously Oppose and Send a Telegram Requesting a Serious Protest

According to Shenshi News Agency, the reporter met with Mr. Zhang, an overseas Chinese who returned from Korea by the Fubo Maru the day before yesterday. According to him, there are no less than 90,000 overseas Chinese in Korea doing business. Most of them are working hard and abiding by the law, but they are still often treated harshly by the Japanese and Korean people, which has led to the increasingly deteriorating situation of overseas Chinese in Korea. However, overseas Chinese are forced by their livelihoods and have to endure their anger and get along peacefully. Who knows that the Japanese Governor-General suddenly announced the Chinese Immigration Law on September 1st, restricting overseas Chinese from going to Korea. According to the reasons held by the Japanese side, they believe that although the restriction measures for overseas Chinese entering Korea have been implemented for many years, the economic situation in China is becoming increasingly bad, which has led to a sharp increase in the number of unemployed people in the country, and the number of people moving to Korea has also increased year by year. Moreover, as the number of Chinese workers increases, Japanese and Korean workers will be greatly affected, and peace and order will be threatened by the increase in the number of unemployed people. Therefore, it is necessary to further strictly implement restriction measures to resist it. According to the regulations, there are a total of four articles. The main provisions are that all Chinese entering Korea must pay a deposit of 100 yen per day, and Chinese workers are absolutely prohibited from entering the country. It will be implemented from September 1st of this year, and all overseas Chinese currently in Korea will also be treated in the same way. However, those entering Korea from Manchuria are not subject to this rule. After the announcement of this order, the overseas Chinese in Korea unanimously expressed their indignation. In order to protect the safety of the overseas Chinese, they immediately convened a general meeting of all overseas Chinese in Korea at the Chinese Consulate General and the Overseas Chinese General Chamber of Commerce in Korea to discuss countermeasures and decided on three points of opposition to this order: (1) The overseas Chinese believe that although the order is only issued for Chinese workers on the surface, its actual intention is to cut off the connection between all existing overseas Chinese and the motherland. (2) It is believed that this order has the suspicion of forcibly assimilating overseas Chinese. (3) China has never restricted the entry of any Japanese people, so it should not hinder the freedom of overseas Chinese in Korea. The above-mentioned reasons for opposition have been submitted to the Consul General in Seoul, Korea, to protest to the Japanese Governor, and a telegram has been sent to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs of our country to report everything. Mr. Zhang finally said that our overseas Chinese compatriots are in a difficult situation under the current environment. It is hoped that the country and the compatriots in the country will pay attention to providing assistance.

Notice from the Municipal Finance Bureau

Levying Land Price Tax in Yinxiang District and Other Places

Levy Starts on October 1

Deadline is November 30

According to Xinxin News Agency, the Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau issued a notice yesterday regarding the levy of the first phase of the 22nd year land price tax for the three maps of Yinxiang District 568 and the one map of Pusong District. The notice stated: "The temporary land price tax collection regulations and the collection scope and start date of the levy in this city have been announced and implemented by the Municipal Government successively. Currently, the land in the Yangjing District 2356 maps, including the Ri, Zi, Shu, Cheng, Tiao, Zhi, Yu, Lu, Jie, Wei, Shuang, and Jin weirs, and the Zhabei District 2 map, Huang Zi, 4 map Ze, Chen, Su, Lie zi, 5 map Zhang, Han, Lai zi, 6 map Shu, Wang, Qiu, Shou zi and other weirs, has been appraised for land prices by the Land Appraisal Committee and submitted to the Land Bureau and this bureau for approval and announcement by the Municipal Government. All land in the area that has been appraised for land prices should pay the 22nd year second phase actual levy of six-fifths of the land price tax. It is hereby decided that the levy will start on October 1 of this year. The deadline for payment is within two months from the start date of the levy, which is November 30 of this year. For land in the Yangjing District, payment should be made to the Municipal East Taxation Office of this bureau at the Chunjiang Wharf in Pudong. For land in the Zhabei District, payment should be made to the Municipal North Taxation Office of this bureau at Datong Road in Zhabei. Those who fail to pay within the deadline will be subject to summons and recovery, and annual interest will be added to the amount owed, and the income of the land will be extracted and sold for compensation according to the number of years in arrears, in accordance with Article 8 of the Temporary Land Price Tax Collection Regulations and Article 23 of the Implementation Rules. In addition to sending the original notice separately, this notice is hereby issued to inform taxpayers to abide by it and pay on time, without delay, to avoid punishment. Those who have not received the notice should, within the deadline, provide the map weir number and hill number of the land and the current address or mailing address to this bureau for verification and reissue of the duplicate notice. Do not delay. This is hereby announced, September 10, 23rd year of the Republic of China, Director Cai Zengji."

Shanghai County Government Investigates and Reports on Disasters

The farmland in various districts of Shanghai County was affected by drought this summer. The county government has reported the situation to the provincial authorities. Now, the Department of Finance has issued instructions, promulgated disaster investigation and reporting methods, and stated that the autumn harvest this year should be investigated and reported by the county in a practical manner, and no procrastination or other irregularities are allowed. Severe penalties will be imposed. Also, the deadline for reporting disasters is September 15. After receiving the order, County Mayor Pan has ordered the district chiefs to report the disaster situation truthfully, and the county will send personnel to investigate, compile the case, and submit it to the Department of Civil Affairs, Finance, and Construction for separate investigation by members. It seems that the autumn harvest will be determined. However, it is reported that the autumn harvest in each district this year has been affected by the drought, and the county's average is at most 40-50%.

Monks Collect Donations for Disaster Relief

The China Foreign Relief Association at 97 Renji Road recently received a letter from monks Yuanming and others in Jiangxi. They stated that the drought in Hukou and Pengze counties in Jiangxi was severe, and they were heartbroken by what they saw. They were willing to collect dozens of yuan from their scripture chanting income and send it to the association for disaster relief. Wandering monks have this compassion, which is admirable. The letter is excerpted as follows: (Omitted above) "Heaven has sent a strange disaster, suffering our compatriots. We have been to Hukou and Pengze counties and witnessed the crops withering and dying. The refugees are miserable. Yuanming and others asked if they had any surplus savings that could be used for disaster relief. They heard the words, wept bitterly, and replied, 'Hukou has a dense population and scarce land, originally a poor place. In addition, disasters have been frequent and agricultural production has been poor in recent years, making ends meet is difficult, and vitality is greatly damaged, reaching its limit. In addition, donations and taxes are heavy, and there is no room for delay. Pledges have been exhausted, and there is no way to borrow. As a result, some families have run out of food for several days and committed suicide. Now that the autumn harvest is hopeless, there is no way to make a living, and they are waiting to be fed.' After speaking, they wept bitterly. Yuanming and others saw this image and were very heartbroken. But as monks, they had no savings and had to donate all their scripture chanting income, and persuaded Monk Zexuan to donate 18.5 yuan, Monk Derong 5 yuan, and Monk Benxian 2.5 yuan. Together with their own savings, they sent it to your association and begged you to allocate a large amount of money to help the county in distress."

There are many cases of selling children and wives, and it is not uncommon to abandon the old and young. There are even suicides in families, or deaths from starvation. Jiashan County has dried up rivers and springs, and there is no drinking water. Starvation and escape are common. The drought in Haiyan and Yongkang counties is extremely serious, and the hunger

The land is miserable. A cup of water cannot save a cart of firewood. At this time when lives are hanging by a thread, those who can offer sincerity and help will live, and those who cannot will die. The dried crucian carp is hoping to be rescued from the West River, and it is really urgent.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Sends Telegram Requesting Correction

Egg Business Tax in Anhui Province

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a telegram to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance of Nanjing yesterday, (omitted title) "According to a letter from the Egg Industry Association of this city, on the 25th of last month, the National Government decided to abolish miscellaneous taxes at the National Finance Conference and ordered all provinces and cities to investigate and ban illegal taxes. When there is a conflict with the provisions of the law or decree, the Ministry of Finance may stop or abolish it at any time. We are very gratified to read it. However, according to recent investigations, the egg business tax implemented by Anhui Province is still soliciting merchants to contract, which violates Article 9 of the Business Tax Law. In addition, Article 4 of the Revised Business Tax Collection Regulations of the Anhui Provincial Department of Finance uses the value of purchased goods as the amount of operating capital and levies a heavy tax of 15 per thousand, which also violates Article 4 of the Business Tax Law's taxation standard. The value of purchased goods can only be regarded as the amount of operating income, and the highest tax rate is 10 per thousand. Now the Anhui Department of Finance mixes the amount of operating income with the amount of capital and increases the tax rate. Therefore, this egg business tax, even if it is not a miscellaneous tax, is equal to an exorbitant tax. Moreover, eggs are food and an export commodity, and it is too late to encourage tax exemption. How can we bear to levy a heavy tax, especially when rural areas are bankrupt and egg exports are declining? For this reason, we earnestly request your association to report to the Executive Yuan and order the Anhui Provincial Government to immediately abolish the Provincial Egg Business Tax Bureau in accordance with the law and merge this tax revenue into the ordinary Business Tax Bureau, and levy it at a rate of 5 per thousand in accordance with the revenue schedule of the sales industry, so as to be fair and in accordance with the law, etc. We have received this and hereby report it. According to this, we found that business tax cannot be contracted by others, and the tax rate should be collected according to the amount of capital and business income. The Business Tax Law has clear provisions. According to the previous situation, the Anhui Province has established a special bureau for the egg industry and levied a heavy tax that exceeds the law. In order to respect the law and sort out the taxes in various provinces and not allow each province to act on its own, it is urgent to correct it. It is reasonable to report the situation and ask your Yuan (Ministry) to review it and order the Anhui Provincial authorities to abolish the Provincial Egg Business Tax Bureau in accordance with the law and follow the Business Tax Law's tax rate regulations, so as to alleviate business difficulties and maintain the tax law. It is a public convenience. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce respectfully reports."

Special Dispatch

Reducing Railway Freight Rates and Developing the Rural Economy (9) by Wu Shaozeng

All of these points are of great importance to solving the rural economic problem. The only way the railway can assist the nation in implementing social and economic policies is by taking this approach. Even if we take a step back and consider that the collapse of the rural economy has complex causes, implementing a uniform freight rate may not achieve the desired effect and may only cause the railway to suffer unnecessary losses. However, it should be considered that the railway relies on both passenger and freight transport for its maintenance, and in fact, freight transport increases, passenger transport increases accordingly; freight transport decreases, and passenger transport cannot but decrease as well. The desolation of the countryside today is known to all and need not be elaborated upon. If it is not rescued for a long time, it will inevitably fall into bankruptcy, and industry and commerce will also decline. At that time, the railway will not only have no goods to transport but may also have no passengers to transport. What losses will occur then? Therefore, instead of perishing together, why not plan ahead and substantially reduce the freight rates for agricultural products, working in conjunction with the government's various rural relief measures, to bring about a day when the dying rural economy can be revived. Moreover, if uniform freight rates are limited to certain kinds of agricultural products, then on routes with little freight, they can be used to increase freight, which would naturally be beneficial. Even on routes with relatively high freight volume, adopting this policy of small profits and quick turnover would surely increase freight volume, which would also be beneficial. Furthermore, this type of freight rate originally contains a long-term policy effect, so temporary gains and losses are not worth considering. (To be continued)

Reading, Questioning, and Investigating Things

(1) Every sudden change, no matter what, is always a qualitative change. (2) Broken glass and a whole piece of glass are always somewhat different in nature. Even if the chemical properties are the same, the physical properties are still very different. For example, the reflectivity to light is different for broken glass. A broken mirror cannot reflect people, which is an example of qualitative change. (3) Rusting of iron is a chemical oxidation process, and violent oxidation is combustion. Therefore, the rusting of iron is also a kind of slow combustion. Ordinary combustion is a sudden phenomenon, but the rusting of iron seems to be a gradual phenomenon. But in reality, it is not so. The rusting of iron is still composed of many small, sudden changes, but they are too small for us to notice. The decay of a table can certainly be said to be gradually formed day by day. But when the degree of decay is not significant, the entire table itself is not affected, and this cannot be considered a qualitative change. Only when the decay reaches a certain level and affects the use of the table can we say that the nature of the table has changed. So this is also a change from quantity to quality. (4) The main cause of the development of all things is the contradiction within the things themselves. However, in the process of development, it must have a relationship with external objects. Therefore, the form of development is determined by external forces. Although the internal cause is the main cause, the concrete development of things is never solely dependent on the internal cause. External forces also have a certain effect. The changes that occur when pressing glass with a hand and the rusting of iron are things that can only be realized by external forces. But at the same time, if it is not glass but a copper sheet, we cannot crush it. If it is not iron but gold, it will not rust in the air. Although there is an external force, if the thing itself does not have the property of being able to change, it will still not change. The true determinant of what can be changed is still the nature of the thing itself. (5) For example, if a piece of glass accidentally falls to the ground and breaks, the breaking is inevitable because the glass has the property of being brittle. However, the event of "falling to the ground" is not necessarily inevitable. "Falling to the ground" is the form of expression of "breaking." At the same time, the fact that it breaks when it falls to the ground will only be realized for two reasons: the first is the mechanical cause of the force that causes the glass to fall; the second is the brittleness of the glass itself. The combination of these two causes is what is called the intersection of two regular processes.
